<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>
<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>
<s> flow of silver to the east    the figures of sir hector hay after 1851    house of commons report    ibid app p <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>
<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>
<s> flow of silver to the east    the figures of sir hector hay after 1851    house of commons report    ibid app p <\s>
<s> 24 are fullest and should be combined with pixley and abells figures for years before 1851 ibid appendix p <\s>

<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>

<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>
<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>
<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>
<s> flow of silver to the east    the figures of sir hector hay after 1851    house of commons report    ibid app p <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>
<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>
<s> flow of silver to the east    the figures of sir hector hay after 1851    house of commons report    ibid app p <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
<s> in what manner does a large expenditure for military purposes affect the operations of capital and labor <\s>
<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>
<s> flow of silver to the east    the figures of sir hector hay after 1851    house of commons report    ibid app p <\s>
<s> 24 are fullest and should be combined with pixley and abells figures for years before 1851 ibid appendix p <\s>

<s> distinguish between wealth and capital <\s>
<s> show that there is no assignable limit to the employment of capital in bettering the condition of the members of a community <\s>
<s>    if there are human beings capable of work and food to feed them they may always be employed in producing something    explain the meaning of this fully <\s>
<s> what is meant by saying wealth can only perform the functions of capital by being wholly or partially consumed <\s>
<s> explain and illustrate the statement that demand for commodities is not demand for labor <\s>
<s> show that expenditure of money does not necessarily increase the demand for labor <\s>
<s> in what way would a general demand for luxuries affect productive laborers and the wealth of the community <\s>
<s> in a community where capital is all employed what would be the effect if one employer gradually withdrew some of his capital and spent this for personal luxuries <\s>
<s> it is contended that    the demand for commodities which can only be got by labor is as much a demand for labor as a demand for beef is a demand for bullocks    criticise this position <\s>

<s> the following problems and questions have been arranged to indicate to the reader the character of examinations set by english 374 and american universities <\s>
<s> they have been taken in each case from papers actually given <\s>
<s> it is hardly necessary to state perhaps that these questions do not exhaust the subject and are only some of a kind of which many more might be added definitions <\s>
<s> define briefly fixed capital unproductive consumption law of diminishing returns effective desire of accumulation law of increase of labor communism wages fund wages of superintendence real wages value price demand medium of exchange greshams law <\s>
<s> explain carefully the following terms productive consumption effectual demand margin of cultivation cost of production value of money cost of labor wealth and abstinence <\s>
<s> explain the following terms real wages fixed capital allowance system margin of cultivation price demand medium of exchange seignorage value of money and bill of exchange <\s>
<s> define supply value of money productive consumption cost of production cost of labor exchange value law of production from land rate of profit capital and greshams law <\s>
<s> define political economy state the parts into which it may be divided and show how they are mutually related <\s>
<s> distinguish between direct and indirect labor and give an illustration of the distinction <\s>
<s> apply the distinction between productive and unproductive labor and productive and unproductive consumption respectively to each of the following persons a tailor an architect an annuitant a sailor and a brick layer <\s>
<s> is an actor to be classed as a productive laborer <\s>
<s> the inventor of a machine <\s>
<s> in which of the two classes of laborers productive and unproductive would you place the following <\s>
<s> 1 the officers of our government <\s>
<s> 2 the maker of an organ <\s>
<s> 6 he who makes an article for which there is no use <\s>
<s> classify as productive or unproductive the following laborers a clergyman musical instrument maker actor soldier and lace maker <\s>
<s> explain fully what you understand by capital and what function it discharges in production <\s>
<s> consider whether or not the following ought to be included in capital 1 the original and acquired powers of the laborer 2 the original properties of the soil 3 improvements on land 4 credit 5 unsold stock in the hands of a merchant 6 articles purchased but still in the consumers hands <\s>
<s> does a national loan add to the capital of a country <\s>
<s> inquire how far or in what cases or in what sense it may be said that a common dwelling house an hotel a school house a police station a theatre and a fortification constitute part of the capital of the country <\s>
<s> discuss carefully the question whether money lying in a bank or corn lying in a granary is always capital or whether its economic nature depends upon the intentions of the owner <\s>
<s> are railway shares stocks of wine wheat munitions of war and land to be considered capital or not <\s>
<s> explain fully whether you consider that united states bonds are capital or not <\s>
<s> is an investment in government funds capital or not <\s>
